Collected Speeches of Rev. Sun Myung Moon
512
Compiled by the Rev. Sun Myung Moon Speech Compilation Committee

Foreword
                   President of the Family Federation for World Peace and Unification  Yang Chang-shik
In the beginning, God created the heavens and the earth with His word, and He intended to fulfill the ideal of His word by establishing the first human ancestors, Adam and Eve, at the center. However, Adam and Eve distrusted the word and fell, resulting in a world of sin centered on Satan. Therefore, God has revealed His word in accordance with the development of human spirit and intellect throughout the ages, orchestrating the providence of restoring the ideal of His word. The fulfillment of God's promises through His word has been contingent upon the fulfillment of human responsibility. This mainstream history has progressed from the Old Testament through Moses and the New Testament through Jesus to the final age of the Completed Testament. The Completed Testament Age is the era of the fulfillment of the word, where the long-promised ideal of God is finally realized through the earthly manifestation of the True Parents, who are the substantial embodiment of the completed word.
True Father officially began his public life on April 17, 1935, after being called to God's providential path through a spiritual encounter with Jesus during a mountain prayer in his hometown of Jeongju, North Pyongan Province. Over the next ten years, he explored both the spiritual and physical worlds, dedicating himself to fervent prayer, truth-seeking, and experiential living, ultimately discovering and systematizing the fundamental truth of the Principle, which is the core truth of heavenly ethics.
Immediately after Korea's liberation in 1945, he began spreading the word and engaged in providential activities for the restoration of the nation and the world. During this process, he endured six imprisonments due to the misunderstanding, opposition, and persecution from established religious and political authorities, walking a path of extreme hardship. However, with the transformative power of true love, which is the core value of the new word, he naturally subdued all hostile forces. In 2001, he achieved a historic victory by being crowned as the King of Peace by leaders from various fields worldwide, following the historic Coronation Ceremony for God's Kingship on January 13.
True Father came as the embodiment of God's true love, true life, and true lineage, and through the history of the word and blessing, he bequeathed these to humanity. His path was one of a true parent, a true teacher, and a true owner. He lived a sacrificial life, wearing the body of a servant with the heart of a parent, shedding sweat for the earth, tears for humanity, and blood for heaven. He not only illuminated profound heavenly truths and taught them day and night but also thoroughly practiced them as an example, consistently living a life of giving with a heart of true love.
True Father's words are an inexhaustible source of life force that awakens fallen humanity from ignorance and death. Since the object of true love is created only by investing more than one's life force, he devoted and committed his entire life to bestowing the word. Although the themes, dimensions, and scope of the word varied according to the providential stage, the conditions of the times, and the audience, the consistent goal was the completion of the providence of true love.
True Father's words have been officially recorded since April 1956 and have been provided through documents, audio, and video media according to the practical needs and conditions of the time. In 1983, a full-scale and comprehensive compilation effort began, leading to the publication of 524 volumes of collected speeches on the occasion of True Father's 90th birthday. This is an unprecedented masterpiece in history, unparalleled in both quantity and quality, and a treasure that will be preserved for all humanity for generations.
True Father's collection of words is the highest scripture, an exemplary collection of sermons, and a public anthology of speeches. Leaders from various fields in America and around the world have praised True Father as a champion who knows best about God, Satan, humanity, the spirit world, Jesus, the Bible and scriptures, human history, and the value of the True Family. Such evaluations are thoroughly verified and proven throughout True Father's entire body of words.
The word encompasses the essence of theories in various fields of human society, including the views of God, humanity, the universe, history, religion, politics, society, culture, and art, based on absolute values. The word is so diverse and broad that it can be said to contain all the themes, large and small, that can be experienced in the lives of humanity today. Its flow contains a majestic consistency or unity, like a great river winding through a deep valley and forming a vast ocean. It is truly like a grand journey of truth.
In terms of composition, the word is a rich blend of spirituality and intellect, religious essence and scientific information, philosophical depth, and literary and poetic descriptions. It maintains a lofty dignity and serene comfort, a passionate fervor and tranquility, and a harmony of sincerity and confidentiality, like the alternation of day and night. The captivating power of the unique language of heart, like magic, leads to constant admiration. There is humor and laughter that makes one burst into laughter, and there are poignant stories of sorrow that make one weep. It transcends time, leading to a sense of unity and empathy that moves and inspires. It is truly the highest pinnacle of human language and the proclamation of heavenly words.
True Father stated that the word is a victorious record of life, a proclamation and declaration to humanity and future history, and the source of heavenly law. By living according to the word, one can transcend the realm of the fall and enter and dwell in the realm of liberation and release, the earthly kingdom of heaven. By becoming one with the word, one gains the rights of resonance and relationship with the same lineage. Therefore, the word possesses an absoluteness that does not allow any artificial addition or subtraction and exercises the stern power of the iron rod in history.
We, the beneficiaries of this providential grace, who have been freely entrusted with this invaluable treasure of eternal value, are truly blessed and fortunate. Therefore, we must strive even more to create a world of peace and the ideal of the word through a life of constantly reading, practicing, and spreading the word. Thus, we must offer infinite gratitude, praise, and glory to God and True Parents, who are the ultimate owners of the word, with the substantial results of our efforts.

1)
The Model of God's Ideal Family and the Peaceful World (16)
(Bow) Thank you. Thank you for gathering in such large numbers. Today is October 14, and here in Seoul, we are holding the twelfth and final rally of this series.
We must unite in heart and mind to leave results that Heaven can rejoice over in this rally. People around the world, who believe in Korea as the homeland of faith, are watching every place I go, hoping for Korea's success and holding a single-hearted desire to help Korea in times of need.
In that sense, please be aware of the great attention and interest in this rally, not only from the world but also from the spirit world, as I am the one holding the records of these matters. Here in Seoul, you are in the central place, so please unite in heart and mind to make this rally a day of record that leaves results that Heaven can rejoice over.
I see that mostly middle-aged and older people have gathered, and I don't see many young people. "Here we are." Where? "Here!" How old are you? If you're over twenty, you're not young. If you're thirty, you're not young. The teenage years are a time of challenges, and we must raise proud young people beautifully and preciously.
Especially young people should be careful and become a standard of hope among brothers, sisters, or even grandparents, and I hope that Korean youth will unite as we start this rally. This doesn't mean we should not greet the elders. Do you understand? "Yes." It seems like there are many older people here.
After this rally, I have to fly to Mongolia. I must travel through all the regions of the six continents, including the frigid, tropical, and temperate zones.
Today's message is "The Model of God's Ideal Family and the Peaceful World." Has God ever had an ideal family? Has anyone ever created a model of a peaceful world? These are riddles. The ideal family and the model of a peaceful world must dock at the end. If they do not become one, the world of peace will not come.
Please understand this, and the explanation of this content... There are many things you are hearing for the first time. There are many things you are hearing for the first time. So, it would be good to spend a lot of time, but since you don't want that and everyone is like that, should I do it for about 30 minutes? Just reading the manuscript takes 28 minutes. But when I set records during rallies, it was three hours and 40 minutes. In hotels, that is possible, but in rallies like this, in sports halls, it is impossible.
So, knowing that, if you want me to do it briefly, I will do it briefly, and if you give me more than an hour, I will do it moderately. Doing it moderately often leads to two hours. (Laughter) So, knowing that, tighten your belts and sit firmly in your chairs, thinking you cannot stand up, and let's proceed with the message.
"I can't hear you!" (Laughter) What are you doing there? Who told you to sit where you can't hear? There are many people, so why complain? (Laughter) I must also give guidance to those who greet improperly. Older people have such habits. Elders, those sitting in the front, please forgive them. Do you understand? "Yes." You said "yes." Even if I speak informally... You're a young person, judging by the way you shout. (Laughter)
Older people should drink water every 15 minutes... Mr. Lee Cheol-seung also spoke well. (Laughter) (Drinks water)
A New International Organization for the Realization of a Peaceful World - Universal Peace Federation
『The Model of God's Ideal Family and the Peaceful World
Leaders who spare no effort for the realization of world peace in every corner of the globe! I sincerely thank you for creating such a full house despite your busy schedules.』
If I were to address each person, it would take all day. So, please be broad-minded and forgive. Having received greetings, let's now move on to the main text.
『Ladies and gentlemen!』 "Yes!" Thank you.『Humanity, having entered the 21st century, is at a truly historic turning point. We are at a point where we must decide whether we can establish eternal world peace or repeat the dark history of war and confrontation that has continued until the 20th century.
As you know, I have devoted my entire life to realizing God's ideal of peace, having lived through the era of constant wars and conflicts, including the colonial wars, World War I and II, the Korean War, and the Cold War between the East and West, which began in the 20th century.』
Since I was persecuted and driven, and in the midst of tribulation, I prayed even more fervently.
『In that process, I earnestly prayed that the United Nations, established after World War II, would become a peace organization that could uphold God's will for the realization of eternal world peace.』
It was a time when I was being persecuted and driven, so I prayed even more fervently.
『However, while the United Nations, established in 1945, has made significant contributions to world peace, it is widely acknowledged that it is facing serious difficulties in fulfilling its original purpose as it marks its 60th anniversary.
Although there are nearly 200 member states, the role of the UN representatives, who primarily advocate for their own national interests, is now revealing inherent limitations in resolving global conflicts and realizing world peace.
Therefore, today, I am proclaiming before all humanity the establishment of a new international organization that can function as an Abel-type UN, alongside the renewal of the existing UN, for the realization of God's eternal ideal of a peaceful world.』(Applause) When we say "all humanity," it includes both heaven and earth.『It has been launched under the name "Universal Peace Federation."』
The term "universal" means "the house of heaven and earth." "Peace" means that two are balanced, and it is about uniting two people and placing them together. The character "hwa" in "peace" (平和) means that everyone can eat and live together.
The term "universal" means "heaven" (天) is two (二) people (人). Therefore, the eternal name that will remain in our Unification Church is Cheon Il Guk! Say it, Cheon Il Guk! "Cheon Il Guk!" It means "the nation of heaven" (天一國). This is a nation (國) where two (二) people (人) become one (一). It is not a nation of one person, but of more than two people! The Bible also says that if two or three people pray together, heaven will acknowledge it, so if two people pray earnestly, heaven will cooperate with the third person, and this will surely establish the house of God in Cheon Il Guk! This is what it means.
『In addition, on this precious day, I am proclaiming a special message from heaven to humanity in this era.』
What is that? It is today's title.
God Cannot Be Happy
『The title of the message is "The Model of God's Ideal Family and the Peaceful World."
Respected world leaders, what do you think is the ultimate purpose for which God created human beings?』
You understand the content, right? "Yes." Then, what does God like the most? Let's say it in one word. God likes money, doesn't He? He likes knowledge and politics too. These are always necessary for us humans, but they are not absolute.
Then, what is the most absolute thing that God, as the absolute being, likes the most? This is a serious issue. Today, we are holding a rally to commemorate peace, but has God ever sat in the position of the King of Peace, as the absolute owner of love? The answer is? "No." Huh? "No!" If there were, what would you do? I say there is! "There isn't!" (Laughter)
Now, by doing this, we have become much closer. We have gathered here, laughing and glaring, but as time goes by, we become closer. If we go a little deeper, we become one family! I hope it becomes like that. It was difficult to gather here, but didn't we all gather? So, knowing each other as one family, I will now explain about God.
God has never been able to act as the King of Love, the King of Peace, or the owner. Why? Because the ancestors of humanity fell. This is not something to laugh about or sit idly by. We must overturn the world and reexamine what went wrong, but humanity has not been able to do that. So, knowing that...
Look. Then, is God a successful being or a failed being? The answer? "A failed being." Although He failed, He must continue the work of creation to rectify the failure. When will it end? When He restores the failed Adam and Eve and starts a family that can live as the representative of the Creator, as the King of Love, and the King of Peace, with God's full authority.
If we had started from there, would religion be necessary? It would not be necessary. Would a nation be necessary? From the family, a tribe emerges, and from the tribe, a nation emerges.
In this way, God is not a God who can be happy. He is in a position where He has no counterpart and cannot freely engage with the environment. How sorrowful must the one who should be the King of Happiness, the King of Love, and the King of Peace be if He is sorrowful?
God Could Not Become the Owner of True Love, True Life, and True Lineage
So, what did He fail in? It comes out today. Here is True Love!
『What do you think is the ultimate purpose for which God created human beings? It is centered on true love...』
What is true love, after all? Since God, who should have been the King of Love, could not become the King of True Love, what happens? He lost the owner of true love. First, there is no owner of true love, then there is no owner of true life, and He could not become the owner of true lineage.
When Jesus came to this earth, did He come as a man or a woman? As a man, right? If He came as a man, what would He do if He came in place of God? The answer that Jesus came to establish the lost lineage is not entirely wrong.
Then, should Jesus have married or not? "He should have." If He had married, what would He have done? If Jesus had children and a family, there would have been Jesus' tribe, nation, and country. Would that country have been a failed country of God or a successful country of God? It would have been a successful country of God. Then, Jesus came to rectify God's failure!
What is the core of rectifying it? First, He lost the lineage. Lineage! Say it, lineage! "Lineage!" You know lineage, right? "Yes." From the ancestors, grandparents, and parents, if you are Kim, there are ancestors of the Kim lineage, and it continues down, but the connection point that allows it to continue is the lineage. Is that correct? "Yes." Therefore, if God is the only owner, He must establish a relationship with the world centered on a single lineage, which is an inevitable conclusion.
Therefore, the attributes of God, who can become the King of Love, have a nature. When we look at that nature, there are many attributes. There are many attributes, such as the hand, the fingernail of the hand, the foot, and the attributes of the foot, but what is the main attribute of God's nature as the King of Love? We must know this to understand the lineage of love that can connect with that nature! Is that correct?
So, He lost the lineage, and then what did He lose? He lost ownership. By losing the lineage, God and Adam lost Eve. Eve was taken away by the archangel. Then they followed Eve and got married.
Then, under whom did they get married? Was it God? Because they got married under the enemy of God's love, the adulterer, the enemy of love, today's world, with billions of people in the spirit world and the physical world, has become a completely separate race from God and has not lived in the completed Adam's family. This is humanity, humanity.
Therefore, what did He lose? By losing the lineage, He lost ownership, and then? He lost the position of parents. He lost the position of parents, and then? He destroyed God's family. Then what? He got married wrongly. He got married wrongly because he lost the lineage. Then what? This land did not become God's possession, and Satan freely claimed it, fighting and staining it with blood. God cannot dwell on this land.
Therefore, He lost everything that was necessary. Also, what kind of sun did it become? Who did it revolve around? Even in the world, isn't it so? No matter how precious the only daughter of a wealthy family is, if there are bad gangsters in the neighborhood and they have a physical relationship, the person who establishes that love relationship becomes the owner. That is how precious and fearful love is.
The Most Critical Issue for God Was Lineage
So, what does it mean to have fallen? Let's not talk about the dream-like story of eating the forbidden fruit, but why did they cover their lower parts after eating it? Why didn't they cover their hands and mouths? What did the lower parts do wrong? What do you think is the most precious thing God created? It is the reproductive organs. Say it, reproductive organs! "Reproductive organs!"
By explaining this specifically, that the basis of love starts from the reproductive organs, we have gained the name of an obscene group. When you look at your family, your grandparents, parents, your wife, and your children, they all have reproductive organs, right? "Yes." What kind of organs are they?
They are organs that require absolute love, absolute life, and absolute lineage. Then, if love and life are poured in, what remains is that lineage continues the history, not love or life. Young people living on this earth today must newly realize this.
Say it, lineage! "Lineage!" If you find one lineage, you find a counterpart, you have a good marriage, and then you form a family, and no one can take away your home, so you can live as the owner. Everything is resolved. The most critical issue for God was lineage! Do you understand? "Yes."
These days, young people think that old people, outdated people, have nothing to do with them, and that the young generation and the old generation are different, but no. The lineage is connected, and it cannot be cut. If you want to cut it, don't get married, don't love, live alone, and throw away love, life, and lineage, and just disappear. It disappears. The problem is that it doesn't disappear and continues to exist. It continues because it has been transferred to Satan's lineage, not because the owner changes.
Continuing with the fruits gathered here, the excellent people, the presidents of countries, the president of the United States, the UN, and everything else, even if they are born from a corrupted lineage, they are undoubtedly children, sons, and daughters born from a corrupted lineage of love! Is that correct or not? "It is correct." Is it correct or not? Clearly! "It is correct!"
We Must Become the Absolute, Unique, Unchanging, and Eternal Love Partner of God
So, losing that lineage is the core of God's main attribute, and what is that core? Absolute love, say it. Absolute love! "Absolute love!" Then unique love! "Unique love!" Because it is absolute love, even God must absolutely obey. It is not something to be done arbitrarily. Why is it unique love? Because it is absolute love, it must become one either inside and out or vertically. Because there is love that can make one, God and humans can also become one.
Then, if you become one with unique love with God, God is unchanging and eternal, so it is unchanging love and eternal love! Since you have become one, you are unique. It is necessary to be unique. Connected with an absolute, unique, unchanging, and eternal lineage, it cannot be separated. This is not a relative relationship but heavenly ethics! Can you buy and sell parents through elections or choices? Neither God nor you can do it. So, you must hold onto that lineage and live until you die. Those who deny it are ignoring the origin of their existence, and such people cannot go to heaven. They go to hell.
Therefore, among the billions of fallen descendants on earth, was there anyone who could recognize God? "There wasn't." Really? "Yes."
What is all this? A gathering of remnants, holding rallies and whatnot, are these God's people or what? Are they connected to God's lineage or Satan's lineage? It's one of the two, isn't it? If they are not connected to God's lineage, they are connected to Satan's lineage. Anyone who says otherwise is a crazy person.
If someone says 'no,' I am someone who says 'yes.' If you want to applaud the first statement, try clapping once. (Applause) You must not do it a second time. Absolutely! You cannot love absolutely twice, and you cannot divide what has become one with unique love twice.

Therefore, He is the only central figure, the Lord! Do you understand? That is why in Korean, we call Him God!

Now, from God's perspective, when you look at it quietly, what did God fail in? The King of Love lost all four major characteristics centered on love.

Now, if you want to become good sons and daughters, you must find that and have God say to you, 'You are my partner in absolute love, unique love, unchanging love, eternal love, my son. Bone of my bones, flesh of my flesh!' Then there is no need to think about heaven. Even without the word 'heaven,' you go to heaven.

Were you born because you wanted to be born? You were born without knowing, and you have all sorts of fantasies with a body like a scarecrow, wanting to rise to a position higher than God. You have all those desires because you resemble God.

Now, knowing that... If I keep talking like this, it will take an hour. How many minutes is it? "30 minutes." It's done, so I have to go. (Laughter) I can't go, so I'm asking you to take an interest. You have to read as quickly as possible.

God's Ideal Family

I will continue the speech on the topic of 'God's Ideal Family and the Model of a Peaceful World.'

'Respected world leaders, what do you think is the ultimate purpose for which God created humans? Centered on true love...' You know, right? True love! Absolute love, unique love, unchanging love, eternal love! With just that one thing, everything is resolved.

There are many attributes of true love, but if you don't know this, you won't know. You can't grasp which branch it is. If you have those four, it fits perfectly. True love, you know, right? "Yes." Absolute love, unique love, unchanging love, eternal love! You must memorize this like a blind person memorizes the Eight Trigrams, whether you go to the bathroom or anywhere.

'It was to feel joy through the completion of an ideal family centered on true love.'

It wasn't made for nothing. It was for joy. But now, there is no ideal family, right? That's the problem.

'Then what would an ideal family look like? First, looking at an individual, we all must become masters of true love.' You know now, right? "Yes." 'The first humans created by God were Adam, representing masculinity, and Eve, representing femininity. They were people of true love,' you know? People who become God's sons with absolute love, unique love, unchanging, eternal love! 'In other words, what was the quickest way to become a master of true love? In a word, it was to secure a parent-child relationship where one could live with God as a father.' You must not miss it. You must secure it. Then everything will go smoothly. It's simple, but we lost it.

'It means living as one family with God.' You understand, right? "Yes."

'Even if you enter a mystical state through prayer and ask what the center of this universe is, you will hear the answer, "The parent-child relationship." There is nothing more important and precious than the relationship between parents and children.'

That's all you need. From there, if you connect the bloodline, a family is born, a nation is connected, and the citizens of heaven are born.

'This is because it is the fundamental relationship between God, who created this universe, and humans.' This cannot be separated. You must find the root and solve this problem. God also needs a partner for love that can give and receive.

'Then what are the characteristics of the parent-child relationship?' Since it is centered on God, the word 'true' is included in everything. True love, true life, true bloodline. Here, it's love, life, bloodline, but it's okay to add the word 'true.' 'It is a relationship of love, life, and bloodline.' Isn't that right? "Yes." 'Without the premise of parental love, our life cannot exist.' Without the appearance of parental love, our life cannot appear.

'In other words, humans were created as absolute partners of true love before God.' You understand, right? 'That is the place where the axis is established, where God becomes the father, and humans become sons and daughters.'

Once the axis is established, everything is over. Then everything, all that is in a relative relationship with it, fits perfectly.

'If there were a higher and more precious position than that, human desire would pursue that position.' No matter how much, there is nothing but that. 'However, there is no such position. It is unimaginable that the all-knowing and all-powerful God would hide the best position for Himself and create Adam and Eve, who are His children and absolute partners of love, in the second-best position.

Our eternal True Parent, God, is 100 percent...' Try it once. 100 percent! "100 percent!" 'He invested His entire being...' General Christians think that if God, like a magician, says 'come out, come out,' everything will happen. No way!

'He invested His entire being 100 percent...' When creating this vast universe, if He didn't transfer everything that was in Himself, the vast universe wouldn't appear. 'He created humans and gave them equal rights,' do you understand? If God stands on the right, I stand on the left, if God stands above, I stand below, equal rights in front and back, left and right, and then 'participation rights,' you can go anywhere. He doesn't say not to follow. And then! 'Coexistence rights,' you can live together anywhere, and then! 'Inheritance rights were given.' It was like that. 'He gave all of God's attributes.'

If you go with true love, the body and mind of all human beings will follow the direction that love goes. Isn't that right for you too? The eyes, nose, ears, mouth on the head! If you include the forehead, all five senses are here. But the only thing that can go in one direction at once, that can go in an absolute direction, is absolute love, becoming one with absolute love and unique love, only then can you be God's sons and daughters, citizens of God's kingdom, and a family of the heavenly kingdom.

'No matter how absolute God is, He cannot be happy alone.'

Do you think God can be happy? What, does God become a judge and send people to heaven and hell and enjoy it? Oh dear! Try being a judge. After 10 years, your dreams will be so troubled that you won't even be able to die well.

'The words "good" and "happy" cannot be established alone.' Isn't that right? 'They can only be established in a place with a relative relationship. Even if someone has lived as a singer all their life, would they be happy singing alone with all their might on a deserted island?'

Wouldn't they be happy? "Unhappy." How unhappy would they be? They want to sing all their life, but if they sing alone with all their might, it would be refreshing, but that's not the case.

'Even the self-existing God needs a partner for love that can give and receive to be joyful and happy.'

If you agree, clap. (Applause) Yes, good! Seeing you clap, you're not dozing off. If you look at the face of the person here before you doze off and say in your heart, 'I am dozing,' you will go 'Ah!' and your eyes will pop open. You're working hard here, aren't you? Think and do so.

'Even the self-existing God needs a partner for love that can give and receive to be joyful and happy.'

That's why He created. Therefore, all things are in pairs, and without love, they all disappear.

The practice of true love is the core of God's creation history

'Then what should humans, as partners who should return joy to the absolute God, look like? What kind of person should be God's child, whom He can call son or daughter, set in an equal position with Him to complete the work of creation, and to whom He can bequeath all of heaven and earth?'

What kind of person can be God's son and daughter, to whom He can bequeath everything? God is not the father of this world; He is the Father who created the universe.

'Do you know where God set the ideal starting point of creation?'

Know this well. From here, the world changes. The root is in the position of the shoot, and the shoot is in the position of the root, so the world has become a world that can only perish and die, but if you just set this right, it can live.

'The principle of "existing for the sake of others"...' Say it. "Existing for the sake of others!" Why was a man born? Why was a man born? Was he born because he liked being a man? What is the fundamental reason for being born? For whom was a man born? "For a woman." Woman! Women, don't be upset. 'The man, like a pig-like thief, turned out to be not the man I was to meet, but a servant. Because I received the seed of a servant, I live without knowing the owner of this world.' You live without knowing, don't you?

'God set the ideal starting point in the principle of "existing for the sake of others."'

This is great. If you have something good, you should reveal it and think not to send it away. God is truly amazing. Where did He set the standard of absolute value? He didn't set it for Himself. He set it in love, which comes when there is a partner. Where is that love? Without a partner, you can never find love that can make you happy forever.

Let's say a word to the people sitting here. Here, Dr. Lee Cheol-seung, a great person, is sitting, but if I ask, 'Where did you come from?' it might be upsetting. I should say, 'Where did you come from?' Which is better? Oh, you don't even want to answer that? (Laughter) Since you are sitting here, you should be happy to be asked anything and answer. You know but don't answer, right?

I'm saying this so that Dr. Lee's roots can deepen and his shoots can grow taller. If you look at the world, is Dr. Lee higher than me or lower? I don't know. If he wants to be higher than me, he should answer what I ask promptly. But when I ask, there are times when he can't answer promptly. So, he is not yet in a position where he can settle and live after crossing the hill! I'm sorry, Mr. So-seok! You liked it when I called you brother, but why do you feel bad when I call you Mr. So-seok? (Laughter)

Now, since we know each other, it's not rude to say such things... Is it indoor or rude? Here is indoors, but it's not rude... Because we are close, we can talk like that and joke, right?

'God set the ideal starting point in the principle of "existing for the sake of others."'

Because God created the archangel first, He should have made a partner for the archangel, but all the love went to Adam and Eve, so jealousy arose. Even children are jealous, right? Even unfallen children. When someone tries to touch their mother's breast, they make a fuss, and if someone eats it, they cry and hit. Our Shin-jun does that too. All children do that. So, the words of the principle of the fall are understandable.

The importance of bloodline

'Do you know what has remained as the most painful resentment in God's heart since the fall of Adam and Eve? Losing the heavenly bloodline...'

This is it. The bloodline was lost. Even if you live happily with your wife, when you die, you think, 'It would have been nice to have at least one child.' You think that, right? If you had a substitute figure, even if it was a woman, you would think of love for your wife, but what is this?

'It was an event where even ownership was lost.'

It's a major event. Heaven and earth crumbled, human history was completely overturned, and God's original creation ideal was punctured with holes.

'Bloodline is more precious than life and more important than love.' Love is something an individual does, but bloodline is tied within the common purpose of the world. 'Bloodline is created by the combination of life and love.' Isn't that right? "Yes." 'Without life, it cannot be, and without love, bloodline cannot be created. Among love, life, and bloodline, the fruit is bloodline.'

It's the fruit. If Adam and Eve were born, they should have offered a fruit that God could be pleased with, but they offered a fruit that Satan could be pleased with, so having given both of the only ones, they don't think they can have the rest. It must be recreated. The term 'recreation' comes from here. Do you understand? Unification Church members!

'Within God's bloodline, the seed of true love is contained, and the body of true life is alive. Therefore, if connected to this bloodline, it is possible to become the ideal human envisioned by God, that is, a perfected personality, and an ideal family is born, and furthermore, God's homeland, an ideal nation, emerges. The peaceful world is thus established.'

It arises without effort. The fools who want to go to heaven, the fake ones claiming to be the Second Coming, that's what they became. Why is there such a fuss? If I hadn't said these things, I wouldn't have been persecuted. God is a sinner too. God is a sinner. He did wrong to humans. Why did He make it that way?

Therefore, He earnestly told Adam and Eve and the archangels to have absolute faith, absolute love, and absolute obedience. How earnestly did He tell them not to eat the fruit of the tree of knowledge of good and evil, not to even look at it or touch it? They should have had absolute faith, but they didn't. Eve, the archangel! They should have had a public awareness, but they started with self-awareness and tried to make it their own, which is the root of sin. Do you understand? "Yes!"

Because of such circumstances, 'It's because of the unspeakable circumstances tied to the providence of restoration.'
